Monday MalaysiaCorporateCourt Top StoriesHighlight KPMG says audit was proper contest Serba Dinamik ’ s suit — company sue auditor
Adam Aziz/theedgemarkets.comJune pm +08According Serba Dinamik KPMG did not respond company weeks informing pause audit Serba Dinamik conducts independent review findings
Photo Mohd Izwan Mohd Nazam/The Edge -A +A KUALA LUMPUR June audit-turned-legal tussle Serba Dinamik Holdings Bhd KPMG has raised questions company sue auditor latter reports possible discrepancies regulators.Depending severity audit issues flagged KPMG auditor ’ s action is guided Capital Markets Services Act.Under Section Act auditors are required report Securities Commission Malaysia SC exchange cases adversely affect material extent financial position public listed company PLC breach securities laws rules exchange.And do so enjoy legal protection employment also be protected being sued PLC.The saga was made public Serba Dinamik May notified Bursa Malaysia KPMG had red-flagged certain bills transactions 12-month period ended Dec tune RM4 billion.After making several board changes expressing plans undertake independent review Serba Dinamik pulled surprise yesterday filing civil suit KPMG alleged negligence breach contract breach statutory duty.Earlier today KPMG said audit was still being conducted accordance relevant professional standards vigorously contest court proceedings.At yesterday ’ s press conference Serba Dinamik executives claimed issues have been resolved KPMG took steps meet clients look alternative procedures determine amount disputed.Serba Dinamik ’ s legal counsel Tan Sri Muhammad Shafee Abdullah also expressed company relationship auditor is no longer tenable KPMG resign.According Serba Dinamik KPMG did not respond company weeks informing pause audit Serba Dinamik conducts independent review findings. “ found infringement law non-compliance provisions ” said Muhammad Shafee
key content is missing KPMG do whistle-blowing SC
result unfavourable red-flagging issues SC acted purely KPMG said raided premises company. ” Meanwhile is worth noting Sections Malaysian Institute Accountants MIA by-laws states litigation auditor client likely deter accountant acting objectively only be addressed ending relationship.This be Serba Dinamik decided sue KPMG instead trying remove shareholders meeting earlier MIA by-laws are said be merely code conduct is not clear given gravity matter resignation KPMG resolve core issues facing Serba Dinamik.Read also Serba Dinamik take legal action external auditor KPMG alleged negligenceNo basis legal action says KPMG Serba Dinamik suit SC says Serba Dinamik probe ongoing auditors do work fear favour Serba Dinamik now says board meet Friday decide independent review scopeSelling persists Serba Dinamik sues KPMG alleged negligence Subscribe Mid-day email alertWe deliver news inbox daily Featured Videos Jun | 06:30amMorning Call FeaturedMORNING CALL Jun | Evening Serba Dinamik ’ s directors resign share price tanks25 Jun | 06:30amMorning Call FeaturedMORNING CALL Jun | 09:24pmEvening FeaturedEVENING KPMG resigns Serba Dinamik ’ s external auditor24 Jun | 06:30amMorning Call FeaturedMORNING CALL Jun | FeaturedNEWS Sunway talks plans post-GIC ’ s investment23 Jun | 08:29pmEvening FeaturedEVENING GIC invests RM750mil Sunway Healthcare23 Jun | 06:30amMorning Call FeaturedMORNING CALL Jun | FeaturedNEWS ‘ KPMG is shoplot auditor ’ Jun | FeaturedNEWS Serba Dinamik maintains wrongdoing Most ReadMost Watched Continued profit growth fails support Serba Dinamik share price

ABC Rural Daniel Fitzgerald ShareCopy linkFacebookTwitterArticle share onFacebookTwitterLinkedInSend byEmailMessengerCopy linkWhatsAppPrint contentPrint images other mediaPrint text onlyPrintCancelAn agricultural development project Northern Territory has had 10,000-megalitre water allocation revoked decision ultimately made Territory Health Minister Water Security Minister had conflict interest.Key points 10,000-megalitre water allocation irrigation NT has been revokedNT Health Minister was required make final decision Water Security Minister declared conflict interestMeanwhile NT Farmers say decision is not based science hope project happen daySo happened Last year NT Land Corporation opened expressions interest EOI 5,700-hectare agricultural precinct Larrimah about kilometres south Katherine.The advertisement described area having unique seasonal advantage crops such mangoes citrus melons time EOI closed February had attracted interest several parties .It also attracted interest Northern Land Council NLC Environment Centre NT sent submissions Territory government questioning water allocation.This triggered independent review then led Health Minister final decision made just last week cancel water licence.Paul Burke chief executive NT Farmers Association described decision being result unfortunate chain events said was first time water licence such had been overturned
scientific data does n't support [ water licence being cancelled ] 's decision 's been made need work ensure does n't happen again future
land does n't have lot potential water
Top scientists not impressedThe NT Department Environment Water Security had spent years doing soil water testing region.Speaking ABC Rural department executive director water resources Amy Dysart said decision was disappointing
stick science department 're confident decision was originally made NT Water Controller said
So are disappointed review outcome are matters process has raised improve address
Based aquifer characteristics … water is available use area
According departmental report Larrimah project have required cent area calculated groundwater storage.Get latest rural newsVisit ABC Rural agriculture mining news including weather marketsSign Rural RoundUp Stories rural regional Australia inbox Friday Rural news daily.Why Health Minister made decision Northern Territory Health Minister Natasha Fyles stepped make decision revoke allocation
ABC News Nicholas Hynes According statement NT Health Minister Natasha Fyles was put charge decision Environment Water Security Minister Eva Lawler declared conflict interest due oversight NT Land Corporation
Therefore acted delegate made decision based advice received Ms Fyles said
transitional zone [ Larrimah project is located advice have been given is appropriate approach likely needs be determined basis specific aquifer characteristics criteria need be more explicitly defined guidance material support Water Allocation Planning Framework
statement chief executive NLC Marion Scrymgour said applauded Minister Fyles decision overturn licence
Clearly original decision made Acting Water Controller was incorrect said
have dodged bullet have had detrimental impacts generations come
had concerns decision was not based best available scientific information be unsustainable long-term – creating risks Territorians

NYSE con una valoración millones Derechos autor Thomson Reuters esta Aa Aa jun Full Truck Alliance Co Ltd FTA subió % su debut en Bolsa Nueva York el martes dando la ‘ startup ’ una valoración millones dólares en la mayor salida bolsa Estados Unidos para una empresa china este año.La empresa que autodenomina “ Uber para camiones ” se suma una lista chinas que los mercados estadounidenses para acceder la reserva capital más importante mundo y evitar un escrutinio normativo más estricto las principales bolsas asiáticas como Hong Kong.Las “ American Depositary Shares ” ADS cada uno cuales representa acciones A depositadas en un banco estadounidense al tratarse una empresa constituida el extranjero abrieron dólares cada una frente su precio dólares.Respaldada por inversores nivel como Vision Fund SoftBank Tencent Holdings una aplicación móvil que pone contacto camioneros con personas que necesitan enviar artículos dentro China
FTA llamada popularmente Manbang su nacional recaudó el martes casi millones dólares al ofrecer millones ADS su debut cuyo precio se situó por rango previamente anunciado.Se espera que esta cantidad sea superada por mayor china transportes por carretera Didi Chuxing que podría recaudar hasta millones dólares en su gigantesca venta acciones prevista para este año.FTA también recaudará un total millones dólares del inversor estatal Abu Dhabi Mubadala Junta Plan Pensiones Profesores Ontario mediante A
La formó partir una fusión entre las plataformas digitales chinas Yunmanman y Huochebang
